            <li class="20180320140546 " itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting" itemprop="liveBlogUpdate" itemscope="itemscope">
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <time itemprop="datePublished" datetime="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30"></time>
                    <time itemprop="url" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html#20180320140546"></time>
                    <span itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                                                                        <meta content="http://www.firstpost.com/" itemprop="sameAs">
                                                                        <meta content="firstpost.com" itemprop="name">
                                                                     </span>
                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="image">
                                                                        <meta itemprop="url" content="http://lbimg.in.com/LiveBlog/img/2018/03/368e4e3b14be8a84d66e0a1053c2e3f8.JPG">
                                                                        <meta content="480" itemprop="width"><meta content="267" itemprop="height">
                                                                    </span>
                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="publisher">
                                                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="logo">
                                                                            <meta content="https://images.firstpost.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/FP-Logo.png" itemprop="url">
                                                                        </span>
                                                                        <meta content="Firstpost" itemprop="name">
                                                                    </span>
                    <meta itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html">
                    <meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30">
                                        <meta itemprop="headline" content="  Two of the deceased were promised salary o../p>

 (In the photo:&nbsp;Santosh&nbsp;Kumar) ">
                                                            <p class="date-time">14:05<span> (IST)</span></p>
                    
                                        <p>
                                                <p><strong>Two of the deceased were promised salary of Rs 35,000-40,000 per month in Iraq</strong></p>

<p>Santosh&nbsp;Kumar (29) and&nbsp;Vidhya&nbsp;Bhushan&nbsp;(35)&nbsp;Tiwari&nbsp;left for Mosul from&nbsp;Sahasraon&nbsp;village in Bihar&#39;s&nbsp;Siwan&nbsp;district in 2011.</p>

<p>They were both matriculates and decided to give up studying and look for&nbsp;labour&nbsp;jobs in West Asia.</p>

<p>Santosh&#39;s&nbsp;brother&nbsp;Pappu&nbsp;Kumar shared that the two zeroed in on Iraq together because the opportunity was lucrative and an agent from&nbsp;Uttar&nbsp;Pradesh convinced them that violence had lessened.</p>

<p>Both the two were also promised around Rs 35,000-40,000 per month.</p>

<p>Vidhya&nbsp;Bhushan&nbsp;Tiwari&#39;s&nbsp;uncle&nbsp;Purshottam&nbsp;Tiwari&nbsp;shared that his nephew had worked in a steel plant in&nbsp;Bokaro. The two were working as pipe-fitters in industrial pockets in Mosul.</p>

<p>In 2014, the two were held hostage.&nbsp;Pappu&nbsp;Kumar shared that the families met&nbsp;Sushma&nbsp;Swaraj last year and she had told them that 39 Indians had been held hostage. The families had been hoping this year would bring them some relief.</p>

<p>(In the photo:&nbsp;Santosh&nbsp;Kumar)</p>
                                            </p>

                        <p></p>
                    </div>

            <li class="20180320134855 " itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting" itemprop="liveBlogUpdate" itemscope="itemscope">
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <time itemprop="datePublished" datetime="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30"></time>
                    <time itemprop="url" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html#20180320134855"></time>
                    <span itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                                                                        <meta content="http://www.firstpost.com/" itemprop="sameAs">
                                                                        <meta content="firstpost.com" itemprop="name">
                                                                     </span>
                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="image">
                                                                        <meta itemprop="url" content="https://images.firstpost.com/wp-content/uploads/FP-LiveCoverage-Box.jpg">
                                                                        <meta content="480" itemprop="width"><meta content="267" itemprop="height">
                                                                    </span>
                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="publisher">
                                                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="logo">
                                                                            <meta content="https://images.firstpost.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/FP-Logo.png" itemprop="url">
                                                                        </span>
                                                                        <meta content="Firstpost" itemprop="name">
                                                                    </span>
                    <meta itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html">
                    <meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30">
                                        <meta itemprop="headline" content="  Gurcharan Singh, one of the deceased, went.. daughter is 11 years old and son five years old. ">
                                                            <p class="date-time">13:48<span> (IST)</span></p>
                    
                                        <p>
                                                <p><strong>Gurcharan Singh, one of the deceased, went to Iraq to work as a carpenter</strong></p>

<p>Gurcharan Singh, one of those killed, went to Iraq on 15 June 2013 to work as a carpenter.</p>

<p>He was 32 years old when he went there. His wife and two children heard from him on 18 June 2013. Since then, they have never heard from him. His daughter is 11 years old and son five years old.</p>
                                            </p>
                                                            <p>

            <li class="20180320133510 " itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting" itemprop="liveBlogUpdate" itemscope="itemscope">
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <time itemprop="datePublished" datetime="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30"></time>
                    <time itemprop="url" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html#20180320133510"></time>
                    <span itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="image">

                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="publisher">

                    <meta itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html">
                    <meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30">
                                        <meta itemprop="headline" content="  Govt was giving us false promises: Kin of ..o us. We wanted him back,&rdquo; Dimplejeet said. ">
                                                            <p class="date-time">13:35<span> (IST)</span></p>
                    
                                        <p>
                                                <p><strong>Govt was giving us false promises: Kin of deceased</strong></p>

<p>Dimplejeet, sister of Dharminder Kumar (one of the deceased), said the government tried to mislead the families all along.</p>

<p>Dharminder, a resident of Batala, Gurdaspurm, was among the 39 Indians kidnapped by the Islamic State in Mosul. After Sushma Swaraj informed the Parliament on Tuesday that all 39 Indians are dead, Dimplejeet told <em>Firstpost</em> the family is heart-broken.</p>

<p>&quot;The government was giving us false promises everytime we met them. Even recently, we were told that nothing happened to Dharminder and he would be home soon. What was the need to lie to us? the government should have been little more sympathetic to us. We wanted him back,&rdquo; Dimplejeet said.</p>
                                            </p>
                                                            <p>

            <li class="20180320133039 " itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting" itemprop="liveBlogUpdate" itemscope="itemscope">
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <time itemprop="datePublished" datetime="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30"></time>
                    <time itemprop="url" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html#20180320133039"></time>
                    <span itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
                                                                        <meta content="http://www.firstpost.com/" itemprop="sameAs">
                                                                        <meta content="firstpost.com" itemprop="name">
                                                                     </span>
                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="image">
                                                                        <meta itemprop="url" content="https://images.firstpost.com/wp-content/uploads/FP-LiveCoverage-Box.jpg">
                                                                        <meta content="480" itemprop="width"><meta content="267" itemprop="height">
                                                                    </span>
                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="publisher">
                                                                        <span itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="logo">
                                                                            <meta content="https://images.firstpost.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/FP-Logo.png" itemprop="url">
                                                                        </span>
                                                                        <meta content="Firstpost" itemprop="name">
                                                                    </span>
                    <meta itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" content="http://www.firstpost.com/india/39-indians-killed-in-mosul-news-updates-punjab-cm-condoles-demise-of-those-killed-by-islamic-state-4397531.html">
                    <meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2018-03-21T09:17:00+05:30">
                                        <meta itemprop="headline" content="  Jatinder Singh, one of the victims, had go..ts in Amritsar. His brother still works in Dubai. ">
                                                            <p class="date-time">13:30<span> (IST)</span></p>
                    
                                        <p>
                                                <p><strong>Jatinder Singh, one of the victims, had gone to Iraq after passing Class 12th</strong></p>

<p>Jatinder Singh, son of Balkar Singh of Sialka in Amritsar, had gone to Iraq four years ago to earn his livelihood.</p>

<p>He had just passed Class 12th when he went to Iraq as a construction worker. Had he been alive, he would have been 23 years old now.</p>

<p>His cousin told Firspost that a few months after he went to Iraq, his family came to know that he was kidnapped. Since then, his family never heard from him. He has his ailing parents in Amritsar. His brother still works in Dubai.</p>
                                            </p>

                                                <p><strong>List of the deceased identified so far</strong></p>

                                        <p>
                                                <p><strong>Opposition making issue out of non-issue: VK Singh</strong></p>

<p>&quot;The efforts were not futile. That&#39;s why we were able to find them...Our whole thrust was to get them back,&quot; VK Singh, MoS External Affairs, told <em>CNN-News18</em>.</p>

<p>&quot;If we were not making all efforts, Sushma<em>ji</em> would not have addressed the House. Opposition loves to make an issue out of a non-issue. Everyone needs to get together to express sympathy for the families,&quot; Singh further said.</p>
                                            </p>

                <section class="article-body section" itemprop='articleBody'>
                                                            

                    <div class="article-full-content" itemprop='articleBody'>
                        <p><p></p>
<p><strong>Latest updates: </strong>"We do not know when they were killed, could be six months back or two years back, in any case search for bodies would have begun only after the liberation of Mosul which happened in July," Swaraj said.</p>
<p>Family members of those killed said that no one from the government reached out to them and they heard the news on television. Sushma will brief the press shortly.</p>
<p>Congress president Rahul Gandhi said he is shocked to hear of the confirmation of deaths of 39 kidnapped Indians in Mosul.</p>
<p>As family members of those killed mourn the tragedy, one of them said that the government had made false promises to the people.</p>
<p>Union minister VK Singh said that the Opposition was making an issue out of a non-issue. Punjab chief minister Amarinder Singh has condoled the demise of the 39 Indians in Mosul and has said that this announcement should have been made earlier.</p>
<p>Thirty-nine Indians kidnapped by the Islamic State in Iraq's Mosul in 2014 are dead, External Affairs Minister Sushma Swaraj said on Tuesday.</p>
<div id="FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_India/FirstPost_Wap_New_India_Internal/FirstPost_Wap_New_India_Internal_Between_Sections_300x250_2" style="text-align: center;" class="between-300x250"><div class="ad-section text-center">
                   <script type="text/javascript">

            googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_India/FirstPost_Wap_New_India_Internal/FirstPost_Wap_New_India_Internal_Between_Sections_300x250_2") });
        }

        if (width < 768 && adKey.indexOf("FirstPost_Wap_New") != -1) {
            googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_India/FirstPost_Wap_New_India_Internal/FirstPost_Wap_New_India_Internal_Between_Sections_300x250_2") });
        }

    </script>
                    </div></div><p>The minister told the Rajya Sabha that their bodies were spotted using deep penetration radar. The bodies were exhumed from mass graves and their identities confirmed by DNA tests, she said.</p>
<div id="attachment_4265897" style="width: 390px" class="wp-caption alignleft"><img class="size-full wp-image-4265897" src="https://images.firstpost.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Sushma_Swaraj_PTI.jpg" alt="File image of External Affairs Minister Sushma Swaraj. PTI" width="380" height="285" /><p class="wp-caption-text">File image of External Affairs Minister Sushma Swaraj. PTI</p></div>
<p>"The bodies were sent to Baghdad for DNA testing. The DNA of 38 Indians have been matched," she said.</p>
<div id="FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS_Native_320x100" style="text-align: center;">
    <div class="ad-section text-center">
                   <script type="text/javascript">
        var width = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        adKey = "FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS_Native_320x100";
        if (width >= 768 && (adKey.indexOf("FirstPost") != -1 || adKey.indexOf("Tech") != -1) && adKey.indexOf("FirstPost_Wap_New") < 0) {
            googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS_Native_320x100") });
        }

        if (width < 768 && adKey.indexOf("FirstPost_Wap_New") != -1) {
            googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("FirstPost_Wap_New/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS/FirstPost_Wap_New_ROS_Native_320x100") });
        }

    </script>
                    </div></div><p>All of them were construction workers, mostly from Punjab, and were employed by an Iraqi company in Mosul.</p>
<p>They were taken hostage by Islamic State militants when they took control of the second largest city in Iraq in 2014. The workers were trying to leave Mosul when they were held hostage.</p>
<p>Minister of State for External Affairs VK Singh visited Iraq, days after Mosul was liberated by Iraqi forces from the rule of Islamic State.</p>
<p>In July 2017, after ruckus in the Lok Sabha over the issue of the 39 Indians missing in Mosul, Swaraj said that there is no evidence to substantiate the claim that they have died. "And declaring anyone dead without proof is a sin that I won't commit," she had said.</p>
<p>Earlier, the Punjab Congress had accused the external affairs minister of "misleading" the country on the fate of missing Indians abducted in Iraq, and asked her to provide "credible information" on the issue.</p>
<p><em>With inputs from agencies</em></p>

<script type="text/javascript">

    function FPgetcookie(cookiename) {
        var cookiestring=document.cookie;
        var i=0;
        var index1=cookiestring.indexOf(cookiename);
        if (index1==-1 || cookiename=="") return "";
        var index2=cookiestring.indexOf(';',index1);
        if (index2==-1) index2=cookiestring.length;
        return unescape(cookiestring.substring(index1+cookiename.length+1,index2));
    }


    try{
        if(FPgetcookie('mc_fp_popunder_v2')=='') {
            var js = document.createElement("script");
            js.type = "text/javascript";
            js.src = "https://images.firstpost.com/promo/js/mcfp-popunder.js?v=20160725";
            document.body.appendChild(js);
        }
    }catch(e){
    }
</script>






<script type="text/javascript">
    dfp_floating_banner_ad_new('FirstPost/Firstpost_Flying/Firstpost_Flying_300x250');
    function FPsetcookie(c_name,value,expiredays){

        var exdate=new Date();

        exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate()+expiredays);

        document.cookie=c_name+ "=" +escape(value)+ ";path=/;domain=;" +

                ((expiredays==null) ? "" : ";expires="+exdate.toGMTString());

    }
    function dfp_floating_banner_ad_new(dfp_ad) {
        FPAdJ = jQuery;
        if ( navigator.appName.indexOf("Microsoft")==-1 ){
            FP_FloatingAd_300x250 = FPgetcookieForDFP('FP_FloatingAd_300x250');
            if ( typeof FP_FloatingAd_300x250 == "undefined" || FP_FloatingAd_300x250 == '' ){
                FPsetcookie('FP_FloatingAd_300x250',1,1);
                document.write("<style> .fixBtm{ position:fixed; left:0px; bottom:0px; width:300px;z-index:99999} .cls{ color:#333; font:13px Arial;} </style>");
                document.write("<s"+"cript type='text/javas"+"cript'> FPAdJ(document).ready(function() { $(window).scroll(function() { if ($(window).scrollTop() > 100) {FPAdJ('.fixBtm').animate({ bottom:0, left:0 },2000);}else{}}); FPAdJ('.cls').click(function() {    FPAdJ('.fixBtm').hide(); }); });</s"+"cript>");
                document.write('<div class="fixBtm"><a href="javas'+'cript:;" class="cls">close</a><div id="'+dfp_ad+'"><s' + 'cript language="JavaS' + 'cript">googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("'+dfp_ad+'");  });</s' + 'cript></div></div>');
            }else if(FP_FloatingAd_300x250 <= '5'){
                var val=parseInt(FP_FloatingAd_300x250)+1

<script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        var id = 'aid_'+$("#main").data('article-id');
        $(document).scroll(function() {
            var pos_high1 = $('.article-full-content').position().top+$('.article-full-content').outerHeight(true);
            var wtop1 = $(document).scrollTop();
            if (wtop1 >= (pos_high1-700)){
                $('.fixBtm').hide();
            }
            else{
                $('.fixBtm').show();
            }
        });

    });
    $(window).load(function(){
        activateOutbrain('4397531');
    });
    document.write("<s"+"cript type='text/javas"+"cript'> $(document).ready(function() { $('.cls').click(function() {   $('.fixBtm').html(''); }); });</s"+"cript>");
    function OpenSharePopup(sUrl, siteName){
        if (siteName == 'linkedin'){
            var sSiteUrl = 'http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?'+sUrl;
        }else if (siteName == 'facebook'){
            var sSiteUrl = "http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?"+sUrl;
        }else if(siteName == 'google'){
            var sSiteUrl = "https://plus.google.com/share?url="+sUrl;
        }
        window.open(sSiteUrl, "twitter","menubar=0,resizable=1,width=600,height=300");
    }

    function twitterShare(url, headline){
        window.open("https://twitter.com/share?text="+headline+"&counturl="+url+"&url="+url+"", "twitter","menubar=0,resizable=1,width=550,height=300");
    }

</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    var hash = '';
    $(document).ready(function(){
        if ($(".refresh-live-blog").length > 0 ) {
            hash = window.location.hash;
            hash = hash.replace("#",".");
            if(hash != "") {

                $('html, body').animate({
                    scrollTop: $(hash).offset().top - 100
                }, 1000);
            }


        }
    });

</script>

<script>
    function activateOutbrain(id){
        var url      = window.location.href;
        if (window.location.hostname == "staging.firstpost.com" || window.location.hostname == "firstpost.staging" || window.location.hostname == "fpssl.live") {
            url = url.replace(window.location.hostname,"www.firstpost.com");
        }
        if (!navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) &&
                !navigator.userAgent.match(/webOS/i) &&
                !navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) &&
                !navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) &&
                !navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) &&
                !navigator.userAgent.match(/Blackberry/i)) {
            $("#outbrainWidget_"+id).html('<div  class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="'+url+'" data-widget-id="AR_1" data-ob-template="firstpostcom"></div>');
        } else {
            $("#outbrainWidget_"+id).html('<div  class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="'+url+'" data-widget-id="MB_1" data-ob-template="firstpostcom""></div>');
        }

       


        //colombia.clearData();
    }
</script>

function ChangeVisibleDiv()
{
	if(Index == 1){
	    if(width >= 768){
            $("#aw_desktop").hide();
        }else{
            $("#aw_mobile").hide();
        }
		$(".weather-widget-mobile").hide(); //display','none');

            $("#aw_mobile").show();
        }
		$(".air-quality").hide();//css('display','none');

     	Index = 1;
	};
}

    });

    // firstpost menu
    $('.fp-icon').mouseenter(function(){
        $(this).addClass('open');
    });
    $('.fp-menu').mouseleave(function(){
        $('.fp-icon').removeClass('open');
    });
</script>
